### [1] [Synthetic Designed Experiments for Diagnosing Vision Model Failure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00832)
*Krisanu Sarkar*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SDRS：用实验设计思想对下游视觉模型做因子敏感性审计，并用定向合成数据修补两类缺口，显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有合成数据常“盲采样”，不了解模型真正需要什么，浪费了可控因子这一独特优势，难以针对模型失效模式。作者希望把合成数据当作可操控实验装置，系统诊断并弥补表示不足。

Method: 以设计实验（DoE）为理论基础，提出SDRS：将下游模型视为黑箱、生成器为实验平台；用分式因子设计系统操控多因素组合，收集模型响应；通过ANOVA分解得到各因子与交互的效应，判定两类缺口：Type I（覆盖不足的因子水平导致的失败）与Type II（对干扰/虚假相关的依赖）。依据审计结果生成“定向合成数据”：补齐稀缺水平或打破虚假相关；并探索按因子不变性惩罚以迁移敏感性。

Result: 三组验证：1) dSprites植入偏置的诊断，SDRS正确检出两类缺口，定向数据将准确率由49.9%升至79.0%；2) 程序化场景的密集分割，发现背景复杂度捷径，定向数据使mIoU由0.948到0.998；3) 纠缠检测显示ANOVA可发现生成器跨因子污染。另发现按因子不变性惩罚会在因子间转移敏感性。

Conclusion: 将合成数据与DoE结合可高效审计并校正模型的因子敏感性，区分并修复覆盖不足与虚假相关两类问题，显著提升泛化；同时暴露生成器纠缠与惩罚项敏感性转移等开放问题。

Abstract: Current synthetic data pipelines for computer vision generate images without diagnosing what the downstream model actually needs. This open-loop paradigm treats synthetic data as cheap real data, randomly sampling the generator's output space and hoping to cover the model's failure modes. We argue this fundamentally misuses synthetic data's unique property: the controllable, independent variation of scene factors.Drawing on the statistical theory of Design of Experiments (DoE), we propose Synthetic Designed Experiments for Representational Sufficiency (SDRS). SDRS treats the downstream model as a black-box system and the synthetic generator as an experimental apparatus. Using fractional factorial designs, SDRS efficiently audits a model's factor-sensitivity profile via ANOVA decomposition. It classifies failures into two actionable types: Type I gaps (coverage failures on underrepresented factor levels) and Type II gaps (reliance on spurious nuisance dependencies). The audit then prescribes targeted synthetic data to address each gap type. We validate SDRS on three experiments: (1) a controlled diagnostic on dSprites with planted biases, where the audit correctly identifies both gap types and targeted data improves accuracy from 49.9% to 79.0%; (2) a dense segmentation task on procedural scenes, where detecting background-complexity shortcuts and applying targeted data improves mIoU from 0.948 to 0.998; and (3) an entanglement detection experiment showing that the ANOVA audit identifies cross-factor contamination in imperfect generators. Finally, we show that per-factor invariance penalties can transfer sensitivity between factors, identifying an open problem for representation-level correction.

</details>


### [2] [Latent Space Probing for Adult Content Detection in Video Generative Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00874)
*Alizishaan Khatri,Chiquita Prabhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出在视频扩散模型CogVideoX推理过程中，拦截去噪潜表示并接入轻量探测器，实现实时成人内容检测；基于11,039段10秒视频构建二分类数据集，方法以4–6ms开销达到97.29% F1，显示潜空间探测在性能与成本上均优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有成人/性露骨内容检测多依赖文本提示或最终像素视频，忽视生成过程中的丰富潜在表示，导致检测滞后、成本高、对对抗性提示/后期编辑脆弱；需要一种能在生成时、低开销、准确发现违规内容的方法。

Method: 在CogVideoX扩散推理的多步去噪过程中拦截潜空间张量，设计并附加两种轻量级探测头（ probing classifiers ），对潜特征进行时空聚合并进行二分类；同时构建11,039条10秒视频的二分类数据集（5,086违规，5,953合规）用于训练与评估；在线部署时按步实时评估并阈值判定。

Result: 潜空间信号对有害内容具有强判别性：在保留测试集上F1=97.29%，推理额外延迟仅4–6毫秒，表明可在实时视频生成中无感知地挂载检测。

Conclusion: 相较仅看提示或像素输出，直接探测扩散模型潜空间可同时提升检测性能与计算效率，适用于生成时的合规拦截；为内容安全在生成管线中“前移”提供了有效路径。

Abstract: The rapid proliferation of AI-powered video generation systems has introduced significant challenges in content moderation, particularly with respect to adult and sexually explicit material. Existing detection methods operate on either prompts or decoded pixel-space outputs. Therefore, both approaches are blind to the rich internal representations formed during generation. In this paper, we propose a novel latent space probing framework that intercepts the denoised latent representations produced by the CogVideoX video diffusion model during inference and attaches lightweight classifiers to perform real-time adult content detection. To support this work, we construct a large-scale binary dataset of 11039 ten-second video clips (5086 violating, 5953 non-violating) sourced from adult websites and YouTube respectively. We introduce two lightweight probing classifier architectures. We train and evaluate it on the dataset. Our work demonstrates that latent-space signals encode strong discriminative features for harmful content detection, achieving 97.29% F1 on our held-out test set with an overhead in the 4-6ms range. Our results suggest that probing the latent space results in improvements in both detection performance as well as cost.

</details>


### [3] [Visual Chart Representations for Cryptocurrency Regime Prediction: A Systematic Deep Learning Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00875)
*Dustin M. Haggett*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 比较不同图像表示用于加密货币/指数的市场状态分类：在8组受控实验中，原始K线图+轻量4层CNN在BTC/ETH/S&P500上AUC≈0.892，优于更大的预训练模型；低复杂度设定（仅价格、128×128）更佳；ImageNet迁移仍带来4–16%提升；用Grad-CAM做可解释性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 技术分析常依赖K线图的视觉模式，但将最先进的图像深度学习系统性用于金融图表仍少见。作者想回答：哪种图像编码、组成和模型最适合做市场“状态/体制（regime）”预测？预训练在跨域下是否有用？复杂表示是否真的更好？

Method: 构造视觉分类任务：对BTC、ETH与S&P500（2018–2024）生成多种图像表示（原始K线、GAF、multi-channel GAF），并组合五种图表组件（如仅价格、含成交量/指标等）与不同分辨率；比较四种网络（4层CNN、ResNet18、EfficientNet-B0、ViT），并考察是否使用ImageNet迁移；进行8组受控实验并用AUC-ROC评估；用Grad-CAM做注意区域解释。

Result: 最佳方案是原始K线+轻量4层CNN，AUC-ROC≈0.892，超过ResNet/EfficientNet/ViT等更大模型；低分辨率（128×128）和仅价格通道优于更复杂输入；尽管存在域差异，ImageNet迁移带来4–16%的相对性能提升；Grad-CAM显示模型关注关键烛身/影线结构。

Conclusion: 对于金融图表的体制分类，简单往往更好：原始K线与小型CNN在效率与效果上均占优；复杂编码（GAF、多通道、高分辨率）未带来收益。即便跨域，通用图像特征的迁移仍有帮助。研究给出实证指引与可解释性证据，为将视觉深度学习应用于量化交易提供务实路径。

Abstract: Technical traders have long relied on visual analysis of candlestick charts to identify market patterns and predict price movements. While deep learning has achieved remarkable success in image classification, its application to financial chart images remains underexplored. This paper presents a systematic study comparing different visual representations for cryptocurrency regime prediction. We evaluate three image encoding methods (raw candlestick charts, Gramian Angular Fields, and multi-channel GAF), five chart component configurations, four neural network architectures (CNN, ResNet18, EfficientNet-B0, and Vision Transformer), and the impact of ImageNet transfer learning. Through eight controlled experiments on Bitcoin, Ethereum, and S&P 500 data spanning 2018-2024, we identify optimal configurations for visual regime classification. Our results show that a simple 4-layer CNN on raw candlestick charts achieves 0.892 AUC-ROC, outperforming larger pretrained models. Surprisingly, simpler representations (price-only charts, 128x128 resolution) consistently outperform more complex alternatives. We provide interpretability analysis using GradCAM and demonstrate that transfer learning improves performance by 4-16% despite the domain gap between natural images and financial charts.

</details>


### [4] [Single Image Defogging Using a Fourth-Order Telegraph PDE Guided by Physical Haze Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00878)
*Manish Kumar,Rajendra K. Ray*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种将物理成雾模型与四阶非线性PDE融合的单幅图像去雾方法：用暗原色先验估计大气光与透射率并生成引导图，再以带边缘自适应扩散和透射加权保真项的“电报型”四阶PDE演化完成复原；实验在有/无参考指标上均显示其在抑霾同时保细节、稳定收敛、视觉质量可比或更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实场景去雾缺乏深度与散射先验且常无干净真值，导致单幅去雾病态与伪影、多解与不稳定收敛等问题；传统暗通道或变分法要么过度去雾与细节损失，要么数值稳定性与收敛性不足，需要一种兼顾物理可解释性、细节保持与数值稳健的混合框架。

Method: 1) 采用暗原色先验估计大气光与透射率，并生成指导图；2) 构建融合物理成雾模型的四阶非线性“电报型”PDE（双曲形式），含：— 边缘自适应扩散系数以抑雾且保结构；— 由透射图加权的保真项以贴合物理约束；3) 通过相对误差范数判据控制PDE收敛与终止；4) 与DCP、改进DCP及变分去雾方法对比。

Result: 在有真值时，MSE、SSIM表明本法达到与现有方法相当或更优的重建质量；在无参考的真实雾图上，FADE、对比度恢复指数、平均梯度与熵等指标显示更好的去雾与细节保持；数值上表现出更稳定的收敛与更好的结构保真。

Conclusion: 混合PDE-物理模型通过四阶扩散与电报型双曲设计，在抑制雾霾、保留结构细节与提升数值稳定性方面有效，整体视觉质量与客观指标具有竞争力，适合作为单幅真实场景去雾的稳健方案。

Abstract: In real-world scenarios, image defogging is an inverse problem due to unknown scene depth, atmospheric scattering, and the common absence of ground truth . To resolve the issue, we propose a hybrid defogging model that integrates a fourth-order nonlinear PDE with a physical haze formation model. We used Dark Channel Prior to estimate atmospheric parameters and to generate a guidance image, while the final restoration is performed via a fourth-order PDE-based evolution. A fourth-order PDE of the type telegraph is then evolved, incorporating an edge-adaptive diffusion coefficient and a fidelity term weighted by the transmission map. Fourth-order diffusion effectively suppresses haze while preserving structural details, and the hyperbolic formulation improves numerical stability and convergence behavior. We use relative error norm criteria for the convergence of our PDE. The proposed method is compared with Dark Channel prior, modified Dark Channel prior, and variational-based single-image defogging techniques. When we have ground truth available, we use MSE and SSIM for quantitative evaluation, whereas no-reference metrics, including FADE, Contrast Restoration Index, Average Gradient, and Entropy, are applied to real-world foggy images. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed hybrid PDE-based method provides comparable visual quality and maintains structural details.

</details>


### [5] [Adversarial Flow Matching for Imperceptible Attacks on End-to-End Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00880)
*Xinyu Zeng,Xiangkun He,Lei Tao,Chen Lv,Hong Cheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AFM，一种针对端到端自动驾驶Transformer模块的灰盒对抗攻击：用神经平均速度场实现单步扰动，并结合潜空间与速度场的协同扰动，既高效又隐匿，跨模型可转移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: E2E自动驾驶正依赖Transformer进行复杂推理，导致潜在共性脆弱性：肉眼难察觉的小扰动即可诱发危险操作。现有白盒需完全透明、黑盒查询成本高或迁移性差，缺乏兼顾效率、隐蔽性与通用性的攻击方法。

Method: 提出Adversarial Flow Matching（AFM）：1）灰盒设定，仅假设目标含Transformer模块；2）学习/构建神经平均速度场（average velocity field），实现对输入的一步对抗扰动生成；3）在生成式潜空间与速度场上协同施加微扰，提升隐蔽性与攻击力；4）面向VLA与模块化E2E AD统一适用。

Result: 在多场景、对VLA与模块化代理的广泛实验中，AFM相较基线显著降低驾驶性能（更高失败/干预率、偏航/碰撞等）且保持SOTA视觉不可察觉性；生成的对抗样本具有强跨模型迁移性，近似黑盒攻击效果且无需模型细节。

Conclusion: Transformer成为E2E AD的共同薄弱点。AFM以灰盒、单步、高效且几乎不可见的扰动，有效破坏VLA与模块化系统，并具备强迁移性；显示仅需知道目标含Transformer即可发动高效攻击，提示需针对Transformer鲁棒性与感知-控制链路的防御。

Abstract: Autonomous driving (AD) is evolving towards end-to-end (E2E) frameworks through two primary paradigms: monolithic models exemplified by Vision-Language-Action (VLA), and specialized modular architectures. Despite their divergent designs, both paradigms increasingly rely on Transformer backbones for complex reasoning, potentially causing a shared vulnerability: visually imperceptible perturbations can manipulate E2E AD models into hazardous maneuvers by targeting the Transformer module. Most existing adversarial attack approaches against AD systems operate under white-box or black-box settings; yet, they typically necessitate full model transparency, or suffer from either prohibitive query latency or limited attack transferability. In this paper, we propose Adversarial Flow Matching (AFM), a novel gray-box attack framework that exploits Transformer structural vulnerabilities in E2E AD models. AFM enables efficient one-step generation of adversarial examples via a neural average velocity field. Additionally, the proposed technique yields effective and visually imperceptible attacks by synergistically perturbing the generative latent space and the neural average velocity field. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AFM achieves a superior trade-off between attack effectiveness and imperceptibility: it substantially degrades the performance of both VLA and modular AD agents across various scenarios compared to baselines, while maintaining state-of-the-art visual imperceptibility. Furthermore, adversarial examples generated by AFM exhibit robust cross-model transferability, indicating that AFM closely approximates a black-box attack setting while requiring only the prior knowledge that the target AD model incorporates a Transformer-based module.

</details>


### [6] [Intervention-Based Self-Supervised Learning: A Causal Probe Paradigm for Remote Photoplethysmography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00882)
*Zhiyi Niu,Xiaoguang Tu,Bo Zhao,Junzhe Cao,Dan Guo,Zitong Yu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种新的自监督范式PCP，通过对视频进行基于“rPPG假设”的因果干预，检验假设是否符合生理与物理预期，从而避免模型只学习到主导但无关的周期噪声。实现框架Interv-rPPG由rPPG提取器PhysMambaFormer与可控生理信号编辑器组成，通过“归零可证伪”和“公理等变性”两种检验机制，在低频色度域精确编辑/验证rPPG信号，显著提升跨域与域内表现，并增强抗运动与光照干扰能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有rPPG自监督方法易陷入“相关性陷阱”，学习到能量更强的运动/光照周期而非微弱的真实脉搏信号，导致泛化差。需要一种机制将学习从被动相关转为基于物理与生理机理的主动验证，以辨别并抑制伪相关源。

Method: 提出“生理因果探测”(PCP)：将潜在rPPG当作物理源、像素色度变化为其外显，基于rPPG假设对视频做可控干预并检验是否满足物理预期。构建Interv-rPPG框架：1) PhysMambaFormer提出rPPG假设；2) 可控生理信号编辑器在低频色度域对视频按假设进行精确编辑；3) 两项可证实机制——“通过归零进行可证伪”(将假设成分消除后是否相应消退)与“公理等变性”(在时移/幅度缩放等操作下应保持一致规律)——来验证假设的真实性，并用作自监督信号。

Result: 在VIPL-HR、MMPD等具有强扰动的数据集上，域内与跨域性能均提升；在复杂跨数据集设定下超过有监督基线；在较干净数据上与监督方法相当但偶有轻微色度残留噪声。诊断实验表明对运动与光照伪影的敏感性显著降低。

Conclusion: PCP通过“干预—验证”闭环把自监督从相关性学习转向具备物理可证伪性的因果学习，能更稳健地抽取rPPG信号、提升泛化并抵御运动/光照伪影，尽管在无扰场景中编辑步骤可能引入少量色度噪声。

Abstract: Remote Photoplethysmography (rPPG) enables convenient non-contact physiological measurement. Existing Self-Supervised Learning (SSL) methods commonly fall into a correlation trap: they tend to learn the most dominant periodic signals in the data, such as high-energy motion or illumination noise, rather than the faint, true rPPG signal, leading to poor model generalization. To address this, we propose a new SSL paradigm, Physiological Causal Probing (PCP), which treats the latent rPPG signal as the underlying physical source and the resulting pixel chrominance variations as its visual manifestation. Its core idea is to shift from passive correlation learning to active, precise intervention: it intervenes on the video based on a proposed rPPG hypothesis, and verifies whether the post-intervention changes match physical expectations. We propose the Interv-rPPG framework to implement PCP: an rPPG extractor named PhysMambaFormer hypothesizes the rPPG signal, while a Controllable Physiological Signal Editor conducts precise chrominance-domain interventions on videos based on this hypothesis. Interv-rPPG validates the physical realism of the hypothesis through `Falsifiability via Nulling' and `Axiomatic Equivariance'. Our editor achieves precise editing of the rPPG signal by intervening in the low-frequency chrominance components of the video. Our method improves both in-domain and cross-domain performance on challenging datasets such as VIPL-HR and MMPD. Furthermore, it surpasses the supervised baseline in complex cross-dataset settings, while remaining competitive on clean datasets where the intervention mechanism may introduce slight residual chrominance noise. Extensive experiments, including diagnostic analysis of nuisance sensitivity, demonstrate that the PCP paradigm effectively resists motion and illumination artifacts.

</details>


### [7] [Towards High Fidelity Face Swapping: A Comprehensive Survey and New Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00883)
*Qi Li,Weining Wang,Shuangjun Du,Bo Peng,Jing Dong,Kun Wang,Zhenan Sun,Ming-Hsuan Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文对人脸替换进行系统综述与基准构建：梳理五大范式、提出CASIA FaceSwapping数据集与标准评测协议，并用多方法实验揭示当前技术的性能特性与局限，旨在推动更稳健、可控的人脸替换发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有脸替换方法分散于GAN、扩散等不同范式，评测缺乏统一数据与协议；既有综述多聚焦于广义Deepfake而非将脸替换作为独立问题深入研究，导致比较不公平、结论不一致。

Method: 1) 系统性综述：将现有方法归纳为五大范式，分析设计原则、优势与不足；2) 基准构建：提出具备均衡人口统计与显式属性变化的CASIA FaceSwapping数据集；3) 标准化评测协议：用于公平、可控地衡量鲁棒性；4) 代表性方法的大量实验评测与对比分析。

Result: 在统一数据与协议下，对多种代表方法进行了广泛实验，得到关于性能差异、鲁棒性与失效模式的新洞见，量化了各范式的优劣及局限。

Conclusion: 提供了统一视角与原则性评测框架，为开发更稳健、可控的人脸替换方法奠定基础；所给数据集与协议可作为后续研究的通用基准。

Abstract: Face swapping has witnessed significant progress in recent years, largely driven by advances in deep generative models such as GANs and diffusion models.Despite these advances, existing methods remain fragmented across different paradigms, and their evaluation is highly inconsistent due to the lack of standardized datasets and protocols. Moreover, prior surveys primarily focus on broader deepfake generation or detection, leaving face swapping insufficiently studied as a standalone problem. In this paper, we present a comprehensive survey and benchmark for face swapping. We provide a structured review of existing methods, organizing them into five major paradigms and systematically analyzing their design principles, strengths, and limitations. To enable fair and controlled evaluation, we introduce CASIA FaceSwapping, a high-quality benchmark with balanced demographic distributions and explicit attribute variations, and establish standardized protocols to assess the robustness of different face swapping methods. Extensive experiments on representative approaches yield new insights into the performance characteristics and limitations of current techniques. Overall, our work provides a unified perspective and a principled evaluation framework to facilitate the development of more robust and controllable face swapping methods. More results can be found at https://github.com/CASIA-NLPRAI/face-swapping-survey.

</details>


### [8] [LiteVLA-H: Dual-Rate Vision-Language-Action Inference for Onboard Aerial Guidance and Semantic Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00884)
*Justn williams,Kishor Datta Gupta,Roy George,Mrinmoy Sarkar*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LiteVLA-H 是一款面向无人机的256M参数轻量级视觉-语言-动作模型，在 Jetson Orin 上实现双速率运行：快速外环动作指导与较慢的语义理解/讲述，并在边缘侧实现更高的闭环频率。核心发现是延迟主要由多模态预填充主导，而非少量解码步，从而通过调度器兼顾高速反应与周期性语义输出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 VLA 在操作任务上具备泛化与语义落地，但难以在无人机上部署，因其需要低时延闭环控制且受限于机载算力与通信带宽。需要一种在嵌入式平台上既能快速输出动作又能保持语义理解与讲述能力的方案。

Method: 提出 LiteVLA-H（256M 参数）并在 Jetson AGX Orin 上采用双速率运行：1) 快速外环用于短动作 token 输出；2) 较慢语义模式用于场景理解、风险描述、对人讲述。通过实证分析发现预填充主导端到端延迟，进而设计调度器在同一平台上并行满足两种输出；并采用知识保持式微调，混合反应式飞行数据、空中语义数据与通用图文标注/VQA 监督，避免语义能力塌缩。

Result: 在 Orin 上，动作分支实现约50.65 ms（19.74 Hz）推理，语义分支149.90–164.57 ms（6.08–6.67 Hz）。与 AnywhereVLA、FutureVLA、ReMem-VLA 等对比，在相同边缘部署条件下，动作分支达到更高的边缘推理频率，同时保持周期性语义感知与讲述。

Conclusion: 在受限边缘算力下，通过识别预填充为主要延迟瓶颈并进行双速率调度与知识保持微调，LiteVLA-H 实现在无人机上的低时延反应控制与稳定语义输出的平衡，优于多种 SOTA 架构的边缘推理速率，同时不牺牲描述能力。

Abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) models have shown strong semantic grounding and task generalization in manipulation, but aerial deployment remains difficult because drones require low-latency closed-loop guidance under strict onboard compute and communication constraints. We present LiteVLA-H, a compact 256M-parameter VLA system designed for dual-rate operation on an NVIDIA Jetson AGX Orin: a fast outer-loop guidance mode for short action-token outputs and a slower semantic mode for scene understanding, hazard description, and operator-facing narration. The central empirical observation is that, in this compact edge regime, end-to-end latency is dominated by multimodal pre-fill rather than by the marginal cost of decoding a few extra tokens. This motivates a scheduler that issues reactive action tokens at 50.65,ms (19.74,Hz) while still supporting sentence-level semantic outputs at 149.90--164.57\ms (6.08--6.67,Hz) on the same embedded platform. To specialize the model without collapsing its descriptive competence, we use a knowledge-preserving fine-tuning recipe that mixes reactive flight data, aerial semantic data, and generic caption/VQA supervision. Beyond reporting current latency measurements, we position the system against recent state-of-the-art architectures, including AnywhereVLA, FutureVLA, and ReMem-VLA, showing that the measured action branch reaches a higher edge inference rate under our deployment conditions while retaining periodic semantic awareness.

</details>


### [9] [Multi-Branch Non-Homogeneous Image Dehazing via Concentration Partitioning and Image Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00885)
*Yingming Zhang,Wuqi Su,Qing Xiao,Yonggang Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CPIFNet，将非均匀雾化图像分解为若干近似均匀雾区域，通过多分支增强与后续融合实现去雾，显著提升对空间变密度雾的处理效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有去雾方法在薄雾且均匀场景表现尚可，但面对空间雾浓度不均与突变边界时效果欠佳；需要一种能针对不同局部雾浓度自适应处理并整合的框架。

Method: 构建两阶段多分支深度网络CPIFNet：第一阶段为IENet，多条支路分别在不同浓度的均匀雾数据上独立训练，得到针对特定雾密度最优的增强子模型；第二阶段为IFNet，将各支路输出进行深特征堆叠与融合，智能挑选并合成优势区域，得到统一去雾结果。训练时以联合损函数同时监督两阶段，包含重建、感知、结构与颜色项。

Result: 在非均匀雾图像上，通过对局部同质化分治与深特征融合，生成高质量去雾结果，较单一路径方法更稳健地处理不同区域雾密度与突变。

Conclusion: 将非均匀去雾转化为多组均匀子问题并融合是有效范式；CPIFNet通过多分支专长与融合策略显著提升复杂雾场景的去雾质量，联合损函数进一步保证细节、结构与色彩一致性。

Abstract: Existing single image dehazing methods have demonstrated satisfactory performance on homogeneous thin-haze images; however, they often struggle with non-homogeneous hazy images that exhibit spatially varying haze concentrations and abrupt density transitions across different regions. To address this fundamental limitation, we propose a novel multi-branch deep neural network framework, termed Concentration Partitioning and Image Fusion Network (CPIFNet), which decomposes the challenging non-homogeneous dehazing problem into a set of tractable homogeneous sub-problems. Our key insight is that a single non-homogeneous hazy image can be viewed as a composite of multiple local regions, each exhibiting approximately homogeneous haze characteristics. CPIFNet employs a two-stage architecture consisting of an Image Enhancement Network (IENet) stage and an Image Fusion Network (IFNet) stage. In the first stage, multiple IENet branches are independently trained on homogeneous haze datasets of different concentration levels, producing enhancement models that excel at restoring regions matching their respective haze densities. In the second stage, the IFNet intelligently aggregates the advantageous regions from all enhancement outputs through deep feature stacking and merging, yielding a unified high-quality dehazed result. Furthermore, we introduce a comprehensive loss function incorporating reconstruction, perceptual, structural, and color losses to jointly supervise both stages.

</details>


### [10] [Selective Attention-Based Network for Robust Infrared Small Target Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00886)
*Yingming Zhang,Wuqi Su,Qing Xiao,Yonggang Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SANet用于红外小目标检测，引入DSM与SAFM两大模块：前者结合标准卷积与“风车式”方向敏感卷积并接CBAM以保留细节与扩展语义感受野；后者以可学习、空间自适应的加权机制替代静态跳连以进行上下文感知的多尺度特征融合，从而缓解信息瓶颈、降低伪警并提升微小目标感知。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 红外小目标常仅占数像素，信杂比低，易与复杂背景混淆；现有编码器-解码器网络早期卷积信息瓶颈及静态跳连不足以区分真/伪目标，导致漏检与误检。

Method: 在U-Net骨干上：1) 设计双路径语义感知模块DSM，一条用标准卷积保留局部细节，另一条用“风车式”卷积获得方向敏感的大感受野，随后通过CBAM进行通道-空间注意力重标定；2) 设计选择性注意融合模块SAFM，用可学习的空间自适应权重替代固定跳连，实现跨尺度、上下文感知的特征融合。

Result: 在概念上可缓解早期信息丢失、增强对微弱目标的语义与方向感知，并通过自适应融合抑制背景伪响应，预期提升检测精度与降低误报率；（摘要未给出具体数据）。

Conclusion: SANet通过DSM与SAFM协同，解决红外小目标在复杂背景下的感知与融合难题，相较传统U-Net类方法更具细粒度与上下文自适应能力，适合低信杂比与亚像素目标检测场景。

Abstract: Infrared small target detection (IRSTD) plays a pivotal role in a broad spectrum of mission-critical applications, including maritime surveillance, military search and rescue, early warning systems, and precision-guided strikes, all of which demand the precise identification of dim, sub-pixel targets amid highly cluttered infrared backgrounds. Despite significant progress driven by deep learning methods, fundamental challenges persist: infrared small targets occupy extremely limited spatial extents (often only a few pixels), exhibit low signal-to-clutter ratios, and are easily confused with structurally complex backgrounds that frequently induce false alarms. Existing encoder-decoder architectures suffer from two key limitations - an information bottleneck in early convolutional stages that undermines fine-grained target perception, and static skip connections that lack the dynamic adaptability required to discriminate between genuine targets and pseudo-target regions. To address these challenges, we propose SANet, a Selective Attention-based Network built upon the classical U-Net framework and augmented with two novel components: (1) a \emph{Dual-path Semantic-aware Module} (DSM) that integrates standard convolutions for local spatial detail preservation with pinwheel-shaped convolutions for expanded, direction-sensitive receptive fields, followed by a Convolutional Block Attention Module (CBAM) for fine-grained spatial-channel feature recalibration; and (2) a \emph{Selective Attention Fusion Module} (SAFM) that replaces conventional static skip connections with a spatially adaptive, learnable weighting mechanism to perform context-aware, cross-scale feature fusion.

### [11] [SparseContrast: Dynamic Sparse Attention for Efficient and Accurate Contrastive Learning in Medical Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00887)
*Paarth Prasad,Ruchika Malhotra*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SparseContrast 将动态图稀疏注意力与对比学习结合，用于小样本胸片疾病检测，通过显著性引导的稀疏注意在训练中自适应裁剪注意力图，减少计算40%左右，同时保持或提升诊断准确，且与主干架构无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学影像（如胸片）在低数据与算力受限环境中，传统对比学习依赖密集注意力既昂贵又易关注冗余区域，影响效率与有效特征提取，因此需要一种既高效又能聚焦关键病灶区域的对比学习框架。

Method: 提出 SparseContrast：1）引入动态稀疏注意力，仅选择诊断相关区域参与对比学习；2）训练期使用紧凑的显著性预测器自适应修剪注意力图，同时联合优化稀疏度与特征质量；3）框架与骨干无关，可用于CNN与Transformer；4）在对比学习流程中以稀疏采样替代密集计算以降低开销。

Result: 在胸片疾病识别任务上，相比密集注意基线，实现训练与推理最高约40%的加速，并在低数据设定下获得相当或更优的识别性能与诊断准确度。

Conclusion: SparseContrast 在资源受限的医学影像场景下提供了实用方案：通过显著性引导的稀疏注意提升效率并保持/提升诊断准确，且具备良好的模型兼容性，适合在小样本与有限算力环境部署。

Abstract: We propose SparseContrast, a new framework that merges dynamic sparse attention with contrastive learning for medical imaging, with a focus on chest X-ray disease detection in low-data settings. Traditional contrastive learning methods rely on dense attention mechanisms, which are computationally expensive and often process redundant regions in medical images. To resolve this, SparseContrast introduces a sparse attention mechanism that selectively concentrates on diagnostically pertinent areas, markedly decreasing computational burden without compromising accuracy. The framework adaptively trims attention maps in the training phase, directed by a compact saliency predictor which concurrently optimizes sparsity and feature quality. This method not only speeds up training and inference by as much as 40% relative to dense attention benchmarks but also boosts diagnostic accuracy by focusing on areas of clinical importance. Moreover, the approach remains indifferent to the selection of backbone architecture, which permits its application to both convolutional and transformer-based models. Experiments show SparseContrast attains comparable or better performance in disease identification tasks with greater efficiency relative to current approaches. The proposed framework delivers a practical approach for implementing contrastive learning in medical imaging settings with limited resources, where computational efficiency and diagnostic accuracy are paramount.

### [12] [Selective Correlation Based Knowledge Distillation for Ground Reaction Force Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00888)
*Eun Som Jeon,Jisoo Lee,Huisu Lim,Omik M. Save,Hyunglae Lee,Pavan Turaga*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种选择性相关知识蒸馏(SCKD)方法，用可穿戴鞋垫传感器数据高效估计地面反作用力(GRF)，在多种设置下优于现有方法，兼顾精度、可解释性与端侧资源效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GRF测量依赖实验室级力平台，昂贵且不便携；鞋垫传感器虽便携但噪声大；深度学习能提准但计算昂贵，不利于实时端侧部署。需要一种既准确又轻量、且能处理时序特征与高维噪声的数据驱动方法。

Method: 提出Selective Correlation Based Knowledge Distillation：从教师模型向学生模型进行知识迁移，基于时序选择的关键特征构建相关性图进行蒸馏，仅保留与GRF估计最相关的时序特征与通道，提升可解释性并降低高维冗余与噪声影响；考察多种师生架构、训练策略、不同步速与窗口大小。

Result: 在多数据条件、评价指标与配置下，SCKD生成的紧凑学生模型在GRF估计精度上整体优于现有方法与无蒸馏基线，同时保持较低计算与存储开销，适合实时端侧推理。

Conclusion: SCKD可在资源受限设备上可靠估计GRF，提升鞋垫传感器的人体步态分析可用性；方法具备更强的可解释性与鲁棒性，为可穿戴端实时临床与运动监测提供可行方案。

Abstract: Wearable sensor-based human gait analysis holds great promise in healthcare, rehabilitation, clinical diagnosis and monitoring, and sports activities. Specifically, ground reaction force (GRF) provides essential insights into the body's interaction with the ground during movement and is typically measured using instrumented treadmills equipped with force plates. However, such equipment is expensive and restricted to laboratory environments. To enable a more portable solution, wearable insole sensors have been used to measure GRF. These sensors, however, are prone to noise and external interference, which reduces measurement accuracy. Deep learning methodologies could be adopted to address these issues, but they often require significant computing resources to achieve high accuracy, limiting their applicability for real-time analysis on portable devices. To overcome these limitations, we propose Selective Correlation Based Knowledge Distillation (SCKD) for estimating GRF from data collected by insole sensors. Our proposed method utilizes selected features considering temporal characteristics in the process of extracting correlation maps for knowledge transfer, enhancing interpretability and mitigating issues in high dimensional data processing. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the compact models generated by our distillation framework through comparison with existing methods. Various configurations of teacher-student architectures and training approaches are examined based on multiple evaluation criteria, utilizing data collected at different walking speeds and with different window sizes. Experimental results confirm that our approach outperforms existing methods in estimating GRF from wearable insole sensor data. Therefore, our approach offers a reliable and resource-efficient solution for human gait analysis.

### [13] [On the explainability of max-plus neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00889)
*Ikhlas Enaieh,Olivier Fercoq,García Ángel*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文研究线性-min-max神经网络的可解释性：初始化等价于∞范数下的k-medoids，训练用次梯度下降；由于输出由单个最活跃神经元决定，提出像素脆弱性度量来定位可能导致分类改变的像素；在PneumoniaMNIST上优于SHAP和Integrated Gradients的解释质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度模型常难以解释，尤其在医疗等高风险场景。作者希望在保持逼近能力的同时，使模型具备透明的决策路径，并提供简单、可计算的局部解释工具，以替代复杂且代价高的后验解释方法（如SHAP/IG）。

Method: 研究“线性-min-max”网络：初始化时将其视作∞范数下的k-medoids；之后用次梯度下降训练参数。该网络的输出由单个最活跃神经元主导，从而可追踪决策链。基于此提出像素脆弱性指标：评估单像素改变是否足以翻转分类，并据此生成解释图。与SHAP与Integrated Gradients进行对比实验（数据集：PneumoniaMNIST）。

Result: 实验证明：所提像素脆弱性在解释相关性、定位关键像素以及计算效率上表现更佳；在PneumoniaMNIST上相较SHAP和IG给出更合乎直觉与更稳定的解释。模型仍保持通用逼近能力。

Conclusion: 线性-min-max网络兼具可解释性与表达力；其“单神经元主导”属性使得决策可追溯，并支持高效、有效的像素级解释，在医学影像分类中优于常用后验方法。

Abstract: We investigate the explanability properties of the recently proposed linear-min-max neural networks. At initialization, they can be interpreted as k-medoids with the infinity norm as a distance. Then, they are trained using subgradient descent to better fit the data. The model has been shown to be a universal approximator. Yet, we can trace the decision process because a single most activated neuron is responsible for the value of the output. Using this property, we designed a pixel fragility measure that determines whether changes to a single pixel may be responsible to a change in the classification output. Experiments on the PneumoniaMnist dataset show that this explanation for the output of the neural network compares favorably to SHAP and Integrated Gradient.

</details>


### [14] [Skeleton-Based Posture Classification to Promote Safer Walker-Assisted Gait in Older Adults](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00890)

Abstract: Falls among older adults are a significant public health concern, leading to severe injuries, loss of independence, and increased healthcare costs. This study evaluates the effectiveness of various models, including a Geometric approach, XGBoost, SVM, and several deep learning architectures, in classifying walker usage, standing vs. sitting, and posture for smart walkers used. Geometric and XGBoost were the top performers. XGBoost achieved near-perfect training accuracy in binary classification tasks, with 99.84% for walker choice and 99.69% for standing vs. sitting. For posture classification, Geometric approach attained 89.9% accuracy for 8 postures, and XGBoost obtained 99.24% during training for 17 postures. Deep learning models such as the 4-layer CNN and Encoder-Decoder CNN also demonstrated strong performance in binary classification, with accuracies above 98%. This study underscores the potential of machine learning to enhance human-robot interaction in smart walkers, particularly for fall prevention.

### [15] [X2SAM: Any Segmentation in Images and Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00891)
*Hao Wang,Limeng Qiao,Chi Zhang,Lin Ma,Guanglu Wan,Xiangyuan Lan,Xiaodan Liang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出X2SAM：一个统一的多模态大模型，将任意分割从图像扩展到视频，结合LLM与掩码记忆，实现基于会话与视觉提示的时序一致分割，并发布视频视觉落地分割基准V-VGD；在统一训练下，视频分割强、图像分割有竞争力且保留聊天能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MLLM在图像级理解强但像素级分割薄弱；SAM等基础分割模型虽掩码质量高却依赖低层视觉提示，难以理解复杂对话；现有分割MLLM多只支持图像或视频且难统一文本与视觉提示。

Method: 提出X2SAM：在单一接口中接收会话式文本与视觉提示；用LLM负责理解/推理与多轮交互；引入Mask Memory模块存储与检索引导的视觉特征，实现视频中跨帧的时序一致掩码传播；统一建模通用/开放词汇/指代/推理/落地对话/交互/视觉落地分割任务；构建V-VGD基准评估视频中的交互式视觉提示到目标轨迹分割；采用跨异构图像与视频数据的联合训练策略。

Result: X2SAM在视频分割上表现强劲（对象轨迹与时序一致性优），在图像分割基准上仍具竞争力，同时保持通用的图像与视频多模态对话能力；在新V-VGD基准上验证其交互式视觉提示到视频分割的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过LLM+Mask Memory的统一架构与联合训练，X2SAM实现了从图像到视频的任意分割与多轮对话控制，兼顾精度与通用性；V-VGD为评测交互式视频分割提供新标准。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated strong image-level visual understanding and reasoning, yet their pixel-level perception across both images and videos remains limited. Foundation segmentation models such as the SAM series produce high-quality masks, but they rely on low-level visual prompts and cannot natively interpret complex conversational instructions. Existing segmentation MLLMs narrow this gap, but are usually specialized for either images or videos and rarely support both textual and visual prompts in one interface. We introduce X2SAM, a unified segmentation MLLM that extends any-segmentation capabilities from images to videos. Given conversational instructions and visual prompts, X2SAM couples an LLM with a Mask Memory module that stores guided vision features for temporally consistent video mask generation. The same formulation supports generic, open-vocabulary, referring, reasoning, grounded conversation generation, interactive, and visual grounded segmentation across image and video inputs. We further introduce the Video Visual Grounded (V-VGD) segmentation benchmark, which evaluates whether a model can segment object tracks in videos from interactive visual prompts. With a unified joint training strategy over heterogeneous image and video datasets, X2SAM delivers strong video segmentation performance, remains competitive on image segmentation benchmarks, and preserves general image and video chat ability.

</details>


### [16] [When To Adapt? Adapting the Model or Data in Federated Medical Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00892)
*Chamani Shiranthika,Parvaneh Saeedi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了联邦学习中两大适配范式——模型侧个性化与数据侧一致化——在多种医学影像场景下的效果，发现其优劣取决于异质性类型与强度：外观差异时一致化更优，结构差异时个性化更佳，差异较小时两者相近。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习可在不共享原始数据的前提下联合训练，但不同机构间的域异质性显著削弱性能。已有工作多从模型参数个性化或输入层面数据一致化两路出发，缺少在统一框架下、跨多任务与多域移位类型的系统性比较与实践指导。

Method: 在六个医学影像任务/数据集上（结肠息肉、皮肤病变、乳腺肿瘤分割；结核胸片、脑肿瘤、乳腺肿瘤分类），统一评测一系列SOTA的数据一致化与模型个性化方法，覆盖不同性质的域移位（外观型与结构型），并量化在不同异质性强度下的表现差异。

Result: 出现条件性权衡：当域移位主要是外观/成像风格差异（如CXR分类）时，一致化方法更有效；当差异主要体现在结构/解剖形态（如结肠息肉分割）时，个性化方法更优；当机构间差异较小时，两类方法性能接近。

Conclusion: 联邦医学影像中的适配效果取决于域移位的类型与幅度，而非策略本身的优劣。文中给出实际选择指南，并倡导未来探索融合一致化与个性化的混合方法；代码已开源以支持复现与扩展。

Abstract: Federated learning enables collaborative model training across medical institutions without sharing raw data, but its performance is often limited by domain heterogeneity across clients. Existing approaches to address this challenge fall into two main paradigms: model-side personalization, which adapts model parameters to each client, and data-side harmonization, which reduces inter-client variation at the input level. Despite their widespread use, these strategies have not been systematically compared. In this work, we conduct a comprehensive study across six medical imaging settings-colon polyp, skin lesion, and breast tumor segmentation, and tuberculosis CXR, brain tumor, and breast tumor classification-covering diverse types of domain shift. We evaluate a broad set of state-of-the-art harmonization and personalization methods under a unified framework. Our results reveal a conditional trade-off driven by the nature of heterogeneity: harmonization is more effective when variation is primarily appearance-based (e.g., CXR classification), while personalization performs better when differences are structural (e.g., colon polyp segmentation). When inter-client variation is limited, both strategies perform similarly. These findings demonstrate that the effectiveness of adaptation in federated medical imaging depends on the type and magnitude of domain shift rather than the strategy alone. We provide practical guidelines for selecting between harmonization and personalization and highlight directions for future hybrid approaches that combine both paradigms. Code is available at https://github.com/ChamaniS/WhenToAdapt.

### [17] [Retrieval-Guided Generation for Safer Histopathology Image Captioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00893)
*Md. Enamul Hoq,Wataru Uegami,Saghir Alfasly,Ghazal Alabtah,Sahar Rahimi Malakshan,Armita Kazemi,Alex T. Schmitgen,Fred Prior,H. R. Tizhoosh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文探讨以“检索引导生成”(RGG)替代纯生成式模型用于病理图像描述：先检索相似病例及专家文本，再做摘要生成，从而降低幻觉与不当诊断；在ARCH数据集上显著提升与真值的一致性，并获病理学家质评背书，但仍有概念混合与标签继承等失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纯生成的视觉-语言模型在医学场景中容易出现幻觉、过度具体的诊断断言与事实不一致，这在病理学应用中风险高、难以审计。需要一种更安全、可追溯的方法来提升描述的真实性与可解释性。

Method: 提出检索引导生成：给定病理图像，先在病例库中检索视觉上相似的病例及其专家撰写文本，再对这些检索文本进行汇总/摘要以生成描述，而非从零生成。以ARCH组织病理学数据集为基准，与MedGemma等纯生成模型比较；采用语义余弦相似度评估，并进行由病理专家主导的定性审查。

Result: 在ARCH数据集上，RGG的生成与真值的语义余弦相似度约为0.60，相比MedGemma约0.47，置信区间不重叠，表明显著且稳健的提升。质性评审显示RGG更好保留与形态学相关术语，减少无依据诊断；但也发现失败模式，如概念混合、从检索文本继承过度具体的标签。

Conclusion: 检索引导的病理图像描述更透明、可靠、可审计，相较纯生成方法能显著提升与真值的一致性并降低风险；未来应针对概念混合与标签继承问题做进一步约束与过滤。

Abstract: Generative vision-language models can produce fluent medical image captions but remain prone to hallucination, over-specific diagnostic claims, and factual inconsistency-serious issues in pathology. We investigate retrieval-guided generation (RGG) as a safer alternative, where captions are formed by summarizing expert text from visually similar cases rather than generated de novo. On the ARCH histopathology dataset, RGG improves semantic alignment with ground truth, achieving cosine similarity of $\approx$0.60 versus $\approx$0.47 from MedGemma, with non-overlapping confidence intervals indicating a robust gain. A pathologist-led qualitative review shows better preservation of morphology-relevant terminology and fewer unsupported diagnoses, while revealing failure modes such as concept mixing and inherited over-specific labeling. Overall, retrieval-guided captioning offers a more transparent and reliable approach with clearer opportunities for auditing than fully generative methods.

### [18] [Dino-NestedUNet: Unlocking Foundation Vision Encoders for Pathology Tumor Bulk Segmentation via Dense Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00894)
*Tianyang Wang,Ziyu Su,Abdul Rehman Akbar,Usama Sajjad,Usman Afzaal,Lina Gokhale,Charles Rabolli,Wei Chen,Anil Parwani,Muhammad Khalid Khan Niazi*

TL;DR: 论文提出Dino-NestedUNet：用预训练DINOv3作为编码器，配合嵌套致密解码器，以提升病理图像中浸润性肿瘤分割的边界精度，并在多数据集与跨域、零样本设置下均优于UNet++与Dino-UNet。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以DINOv3为编码器，设计Nested Dense Decoder：构建致密的中间路径网格，进行连续特征复用与多尺度再校准；用致密跳连替代稀疏skip与线性上采样，使高层语义与低层形态在解码过程中逐步对齐。与UNet++和Dino-UNet对比，在多病理队列与跨域设置评估，并进行基于CHTN训练、在TIGER WSIBULK与OSU CRC上的零样本测试。

Result: 在CHTN、OSU、CAMELYON16上取得一致优于UNet++与标准Dino-UNet的性能提升，跨域迁移时提升更明显；零样本从CHTN直接测试到TIGER WSIBULK与OSU CRC依然保持优势，显示更强外部泛化。

Conclusion: 解码端的致密重建与多尺度对齐是释放基础编码器能力、提升边界敏感病理分割的关键；Dino-NestedUNet在多域和零样本条件下验证了该设计的有效性。

Abstract: Vision foundation models (VFMs), such as DINOv3, provide rich semantic representations that are promising for computational pathology. However, many current adaptations pair frozen VFMs with lightweight decoders, creating a capacity mismatch that often limits boundary fidelity for infiltrative tumor bulk segmentation. This paper presents Dino-NestedUNet, a framework that couples a pre-trained DINOv3 encoder with a Nested Dense Decoder. Instead of sparse skip connections and linear upsampling, the proposed decoder forms a dense grid of intermediate pathways to enable continuous feature reuse and multi-scale recalibration, aligning high-level semantics with low-level morphological textures during reconstruction. We evaluate Dino-NestedUNet on three histopathology cohorts (multi-center CHTN, institutional OSU, and CAMELYON16) and observe consistent improvements over UNet++ and standard Dino-UNet variants, particularly under cross-domain shift. To further assess external generalization, we perform zero-shot evaluation by training on CHTN and directly testing on unseen TIGER WSIBULK and OSU CRC cohorts without fine-tuning. These results suggest that dense decoding is a key ingredient for unlocking foundation encoders in boundary-sensitive pathology segmentation.

### [19] [When Less Is More: Simplicity Beats Complexity for Physics-Constrained InSAR Phase Unwrapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00896)
*Prabhjot Singh,Manmeet Singh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文通过大规模基准测试表明，在InSAR相位展开这一受物理约束的平滑场回归任务中，简单的卷积式U-Net在精度、速度与稳定性上显著优于更复杂的注意力模型，且注意力会引入不物理的高频伪影。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 运维级InSAR火山/地震监测的主要计算瓶颈是相位展开。业界趋势偏好引入高复杂度的计算机视觉架构（如注意力），但缺乏其在受物理约束的地球物理回归任务中的适配性验证。作者希望系统检验复杂度是否真的带来收益，避免“从发表到落地”的落差。

Method: 在全球LiCSAR基准上进行首个大规模架构消融：20帧、39,724个patch、6.51亿像素。对比 vanilla U-Net 与多种含注意力的模型，评估R^2、RMSE、推理时延，并用功率谱密度（PSD）分析输出频谱，检验与弹性形变的平滑性物理先验是否一致。

Result: vanilla U-Net（7.76M参数）取得R^2=0.834、RMSE=1.01 cm，较11.37M参数的注意力模型分别提升34%（R^2）与51%（RMSE）。注意力模型在>0.3 cycles/pixel处产生不物理高频伪影。U-Net推理延迟2.92ms，实现约2.5×加速，是唯一可轻松满足<100ms早预警需求的模型。

Conclusion: 在平滑场的地球物理回归中，卷积的局部性与物理先验更契合；增加架构复杂度（如注意力）不仅无益，反而带来“复杂度罚分”。应倡导物理启发的简约模型以实现可靠、可部署的ML4RS。

Abstract: Operational phase unwrapping is the primary computational bottleneck in InSAR-based volcanic and seismic monitoring. We challenge the industry trend of adopting high-complexity computer vision architectures, such as attention mechanisms, without validating their suitability for physics-constrained geophysical regression. We present the first large-scale architectural ablation study on a global LiCSAR benchmark (20 frames, 39,724 patches, 651M pixels). Our results reveal a significant "complexity penalty": a vanilla U-Net (7.76M parameters) achieves $R^2=0.834$ and RMSE $= 1.01$ cm, outperforming 11.37M-parameter attention-based models by 34% in $R^2$ and 51% in RMSE. Power Spectral Density (PSD) analysis provides the physical justification: while attention excels at capturing sharp semantic edges in natural images, it injects unphysical high-frequency artifacts ($>0.3$ cycles/pixel) into geophysical fields, violating the fundamental smoothness constraints of elastic surface deformation. With a 2.92ms inference latency (a $2.5\times$ speedup), the vanilla U-Net is the only candidate to comfortably meet the sub-100ms requirement for operational early-warning systems. This work bridges the "publication-to-practice" gap by proving that convolutional locality outperforms modern complexity for smooth-field regression, advocating for physics-informed simplicity in ML4RS. Code available at https://github.com/prabhjotschugh/When-Less-is-More-InSAR-Phase-Unwrapping

### [20] [LatentDiff: Scaling Semantic Dataset Comparison to Millions of Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00899)
*James Flora,Kowshik Thopalli,Akshay R. Kulkarni,Weng-Keen Wong,Shusen Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LatentDiff在预训练视觉编码器的潜在空间中比较数据集，结合稀疏自编码器的散度检测与密度比估计，以低成本发现可解释的语义差异；并提出包含稀疏分布漂移的Noisy-Diff基准；在仅有5%到<1%差异时仍具高准确与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有依赖文本描述/标注（如caption）的数据集比较方法计算昂贵、易受噪声影响，且难以在稀疏语义漂移场景中稳定工作。作者希望直接在视觉潜在空间中检测与定位语义差异，以提升效率、可解释性与在稀疏差异下的检出能力。

Method: 1) 使用预训练视觉编码器将图像映射到潜在空间；2) 基于稀疏自编码器（SAE）构建可解释特征，并进行分布散度/差异检验以定位哪些稀疏特征在两个数据集间发生变化；3) 结合密度比估计以量化差异强度与方向；4) 形成LatentDiff框架实现可扩展的语义比较。另提出Noisy-Diff基准，模拟现实中稀疏且细粒度的分布漂移。

Result: 在包含稀疏分布变化（5%到<1%样本差异）的实验中，LatentDiff相较基于caption的替代方法以更低计算成本达到更高精度，并在多种设置下保持鲁棒；在Noisy-Diff基准上也优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 直接在潜在空间进行比较、结合SAE散度检测与密度比估计可高效、可解释地发现跨数据集的语义差异；该方法在极稀疏差异场景下依然有效，并通过新基准验证其实用性与优势。

Abstract: We present LatentDiff, a scalable framework for semantic dataset comparison that operates directly in the latent space of pretrained vision encoders. By combining sparse autoencoder-based divergence testing with density ratio estimation, LatentDiff identifies interpretable semantic differences between datasets at a fraction of the computational cost of caption-based alternatives. We also introduce Noisy-Diff, a benchmark capturing realistic sparse distribution shifts that cause existing methods to struggle. Experiments demonstrate that LatentDiff achieves superior accuracy while remaining robust to settings where an extremely small fraction of images (from 5% to <1% ) differ semantically.

### [21] [RA-CMF: Region-Adaptive Conditional MeanFlow for CT Image Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00901)
*Md Shifatul Ahsan Apurba,Md Selim,Jin Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种结合条件MeanFlow与强化学习策略网络的CT图像重建与增强方法，针对跨设备/协议带来的噪声、对比度与纹理差异，实现自适应、区域化的迭代增强与计算预算分配，显著提升肿瘤ROI与整体图像质量（高CCC、PSNR与SSIM）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨中心/扫描仪的CT存在噪声统计、对比度与纹理不一致，影响肺癌筛查、诊断与疗效评估中重建与放射组学稳定性；需要一种既能统一增强轨迹、又能在空间上自适应分配计算与停止准则的重建方案，以在难区强化、易区稳定的同时控制计算成本与避免不稳定。

Method: 1) 条件MeanFlow网络：将图像增强建模为从中间状态到目标状态的条件流场预测，联合MeanFlow一致性损失与重建损失进行训练；2) 区域强化学习策略网络：根据MeanFlow rollout信息，按图块预测细化预算、停止准则与总预算分配；采用基于策略梯度的奖励，鼓励质量提升、惩罚冗余计算与不稳定；3) 二者结合实现条件流增强+RL空间控制的自适应重建流程。

Conclusion: 所提方法通过条件流增强与强化学习的区域预算控制，实现对困难区域的重点提升与对已良好区域的稳定与早停，兼顾精度与效率，改善跨设备/协议下CT重建一致性与放射组学可靠性。

Abstract: The use of CT imaging is important for screening, diagnosis, therapy planning, and prognosis of lung cancers. Unfortunately, due to differences in imaging protocols and scanner models, CT images acquired by different means may show large differences in noise statistics, contrast, and texture. In this study, we develop a novel conditional MeanFlow pipeline for CT image reconstruction. We introduce a conditional MeanFlow network that models the enhancement trajectory by predicting image-conditioned flow fields given intermediate image states. The image enhancement network is trained with a MeanFlow consistency loss along with the image reconstruction loss. In order to provide an adaptive refinement process in terms of spatial location of enhancements, we integrate a regional reinforcement learning-driven policy network into our approach. The policy network receives information about the MeanFlow rollouts and provides predictions in terms of tile-wise refinement budgets, stopping criteria, and total budget allocation of enhancement processes. Our policy network is trained through reinforcement learning in a policy gradient framework, where the goal of the training reward is to maximize improvement of enhancements while minimizing unnecessary computations and avoiding instabilities. In this way, our approach combines conditional flow-based enhancement with reinforcement learning-based spatial enhancement control. This allows our approach to focus more attention on enhancing difficult areas while stabilizing areas already showing sufficient quality. Our results show high accuracy in the tumor ROI, with the average radiomic feature CCC being 0.96, an average PSNR of 31.30 $\pm$ 4.16, and average SSIM of 0.94 $\pm$ 0.07. Moreover, there is an improvement in the overall quality of images, with an average PSNR of 34.23 $\pm$ 1.71 and average SSIM of 0.95 $\pm$ 0.01.

### [22] [Validation of Whole-Slide Foundation Models for Image Retrieval in TCGA Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00902)
*Tianhao Lei,Parsa Esmaeilkhani,Saghir Alfasly,Wataru Uegami,Judy C. Boughey,Matthew P. Goetz,Krishna R. Kalari,H. R. Tizhoosh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 在TCGA 9,387张全切片的检索任务中，对比4个切片级基础模型、ABMIL聚合与多密度补丁级检索。总体差异主要来自器官/诊断而非架构；TITAN略优但优势有限，ABMIL与补丁检索相当，无一统治。形态显著实体接近天花板，稀有/异质/近缘亚型困难且部分为0%准确。补丁特征决定性能，切片级聚合收益有限。最佳模型仅约68%±21%准确，提示形态学检索存在内在上限，需更强特征、多模态与器官/诊断感知策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基础模型在病理学中崛起，但其在全切片检索任务相对于强大的补丁级与监督聚合基线的真实增益尚不明确；需要系统基准来判断是否存在通用最优架构与当前方法的临床可用性。

Method: 在TCGA 17个器官、60个诊断的9,387张诊断性WSI上，以病人级留一交叉评估对比10条管线：4个预训练切片基础模型、使用补丁嵌入的监督ABMIL聚合，以及5种采样密度的补丁级检索。衡量Top-1/Top-3准确率，并按器官/诊断细分分析错误与上限。

Result: 性能在器官/诊断间波动大于在架构间；TITAN总体最佳但优势温和，ABMIL与补丁方法可达相近Top-1/Top-3且无方法稳定领先。形态独特实体接近天花板；稀有、异质、近缘亚型困难，部分子类型在所有方法上为0%准确。误判集中于已知观察者差异大的器官，暗示形态学检索存在内在上限。总体最佳准确率约68%±21%。

Conclusion: 不存在普适最优架构；性能主要由补丁级特征决定，许多情景下切片级聚合可能非必需。应进行器官分辨的基准、诊断感知或集成策略、强化特征表示，并引入多模态检索。形态学表示存在根本局限，当前方法距离可靠临床部署仍有显著差距。

Abstract: Foundation models are reshaping computational histopathology, yet their value for whole-slide image retrieval relative to strong patch-based and supervised aggregation baselines remains unclear. We benchmarked ten pipelines on 9,387 diagnostic slides spanning 17 organs and 60 diagnoses from The Cancer Genome Atlas (TCGA) using patient-level leave-one-patient-out evaluation. Methods included four pre-trained slide foundation models, a supervised attention-based multiple instance learning (ABMIL) aggregator on patch embeddings, and patch-level retrieval across five sampling densities.
  Performance varied more across organs and diagnoses than across architectures. Although the slide foundation model TITAN achieved the strongest overall results, its advantage was modest; ABMIL and patch-based methods reached comparable Top-1 and Top-3 accuracy, with no model consistently dominant. Morphologically distinctive entities approached ceiling performance, while rare, heterogeneous, and closely related subtypes remained challenging. Misclassifications aligned with organs exhibiting known inter-observer variability, suggesting an intrinsic ceiling for morphology-only retrieval.
  Performance was driven primarily by patch-level feature representations, with limited benefit from slide-level aggregation, indicating aggregation may be unnecessary in many settings. These findings argue against a universally optimal architecture and instead support organ-resolved benchmarking, diagnosis-aware or ensemble strategies, stronger feature representations, and multimodal retrieval frameworks. Notably, even the best model achieved only $\approx 68\% \pm 21\%$ retrieval accuracy on TCGA, and some subtypes showed $0\%$ accuracy across all methods, highlighting fundamental limitations of morphology-based representations and the need for substantial progress before reliable clinical deployment.

</details>

### [24] [Robustness of Transformer-Based Fluence Map Prediction Under Clinically Realistic Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00904)
*Ujunwa Mgboh,Rafi Ibn Sultan,Joshua Kim,Kundan Thind,Dongxiao Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 研究评估一种两阶段Transformer从解剖到剂量、再到光子束元流强图（fluence）的IMRT快速预测方法在分布偏移下的稳健性，发现适度扰动下性能平滑下降，但在严重旋转与噪声下会失效；分层Transformer更稳健，且仅用SSIM会漏掉临床关键误差，物理约束与评估必不可少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 迭代逆向规划计算昂贵、耗时，难以在临床快速决策与自适应放疗中应用；学习式流强预测虽快，但其在现实世界的几何/成像/数据分布变化下的鲁棒性与临床可靠性未被系统量化。

Method: 提出两阶段管线：(1) Anatomy→Dose 的Transformer（用CT及勾画的器官/靶区）；(2) Dose→Fluence 的Transformer。比较分层、全局与混合注意力骨干，并引入物理启发损失以约束能量守恒/一致性。基于前列腺IMRT数据，在几何扰动（旋转/位移）、辐射/成像噪声、训练数据缩减与跨域迁移下评估鲁棒性；并在公共数据集上额外评估剂量阶段。

Result: 在中等强度扰动下性能随扰动强度平滑下降；但在严重旋转和高噪声下出现明显失败（能量误差与预测失真激增）。分层Transformer（如SwinUNETR）上四分位能量误差增长更慢，鲁棒性更好。发现仅用SSIM会漏检对临床重要的错误。

Conclusion: 两阶段Transformer在温和分布偏移下可用，但对强旋转/噪声敏感；分层注意力结构更稳健。评估与训练需纳入物理一致性指标，单纯依赖图像相似度（SSIM）不足，应采用物理约束与临床相关误差度量以提升可靠性。

Abstract: Learning-based fluence map prediction offers a fast alternative to iterative inverse planning in intensity-modulated radiation therapy (IMRT), but its robustness under realistic distribution shifts remains unclear. We study a two-stage transformer pipeline that maps anatomy (CT and contours) to dose and then to beamlet fluence maps. We compare fluence-stage transformer backbones with hierarchical, global, and hybrid attention, trained with a physics-informed loss enforcing energy consistency. Robustness is evaluated under geometric perturbations, radiometric noise, reduced training data, and domain shifts using a prostate IMRT dataset, with additional evaluation of the dose stage on public datasets. Results show smooth degradation under moderate perturbations but sharp failures under severe rotations and noise. Hierarchical transformers (e.g., SwinUNETR) exhibit slower growth in upper-quartile energy error, indicating improved robustness. We further show that SSIM alone fails to capture clinically relevant errors, highlighting the need for physics-informed evaluation.

### [25] [Generalized Category Discovery under Domain Shifts: From Vision to Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00906)
*Hongjun Wang,Po Hu,Kai Han*

Main category: cs.CV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实未标注数据同时存在语义漂移与领域漂移，而现有GCD方法假定单一域，难以泛化。需要能在域移条件下把已知类知识迁移到未知类并稳健聚类/分类的通用框架。

Method: 在不同基础骨干上设计三套方法但共享原则：
- HiLo：多层级特征提取，最小化域与语义特征的互信息以解耦；结合PatchMix数据增强与课程式采样，稳健学习。
- HLPrompt：在HiLo之上，对视觉基础模型做语义感知的空间Prompt调优，抑制背景与域噪声。
- VLPrompt：利用视觉-语言模型，采用因子化文本提示并进行跨模态一致性正则，提升已知/未知类分辨与跨域泛化。

Result: 在合成腐化与真实多域数据集上，三种方法均对强基线取得一致而显著的性能提升，验证其鲁棒性与泛化能力。

Conclusion: 通过在基础模型上引入域-语义解耦、语义空间提示与跨模态一致性，GCD在域移场景下得到稳健提升；三种方案适配不同部署需求并具有广泛适用性。

Abstract: Generalized Category Discovery (GCD) aims to categorize unlabelled instances from both known and unknown classes by transferring knowledge from labelled data of known classes. Existing methods assume all data comes from a single domain, yet real-world unlabelled data often exhibits domain shifts alongside semantic shifts. We study GCD under domain shifts and propose three frameworks that adapt foundation models, ranging from self-supervised vision models to vision-language models. (i) HiLo disentangles domain and semantic features through multi-level feature extraction and mutual information minimization, combined with PatchMix augmentation and curriculum sampling. (ii) HLPrompt extends HiLo with semantic-aware spatial prompt tuning to suppress background and domain noise. (iii) VLPrompt leverages vision-language models via factorized textual prompts and cross-modal consistency regularization. The three methods share core design principles while operating on different foundation backbones, making them suitable for different deployment scenarios. Extensive experiments on synthetic corruptions and real-world multi-domain shifts demonstrate consistent improvements over strong baselines. Project page: https://visual-ai.github.io/hilo/

Method: 提出 TRIP-Evaluate：按角色-任务-知识的分类法组织837道题，覆盖车辆、交通管理、出行者、规划与设计功能，并为每题标注能力、模态、难度标签以支持从总体到失效模式的诊断；同时标准化题目构建、质检、提示词、解码与评分流程，提升跨模型可比性。数据构成包含596文本、198图像、43点云项目。

Conclusion: TRIP-Evaluate 提供可复现实验、可诊断分析、贴近工程应用的评测基线，可用于模型选型、回归测试与更安全的交通领域部署。

Yet transportation workflows are rule-intensive, computation-intensive, safety-critical, and inherently multimodal. Existing general benchmarks provide limited evidence of whether a model can apply regulations correctly, perform verifiable engineering calculations, or interpret traffic scenes reliably, while the small number of public transportation benchmarks remain narrow in scope and rarely support fine-grained diagnosis across text, images, and point-cloud data. To address this gap, we present TRIP-Evaluate, an open multimodal benchmark for large models in transportation. The benchmark organizes 837 items using a role-task-knowledge taxonomy that covers vehicle, traffic-management, traveler, and planning-and-design functions. Each item is annotated with capability, modality, and difficulty labels, enabling diagnosis from overall accuracy down to specific failure modes. The current release includes 596 text items, 198 image items, and 43 point-cloud items. TRIP-Evaluate also standardizes item construction, quality control, prompting, decoding, and scoring to improve cross-model comparability. Results on a diverse panel of models show that text-based performance is improving, but substantial weaknesses remain in multi-step engineering calculation, rule-constrained reasoning, multimodal scene understanding, and point-cloud understanding. Overall, TRIP-Evaluate provides a reproducible, diagnosable, and engineering-aligned evaluation baseline for model selection, regression testing, and safer deployment in transportation applications.

Abstract: This paper presents a comparative evaluation of convolutional and transformer-based object detection architectures for early weed detection in realistic scenarios. Experiments were conducted on the GROUNDBASED_ WEED dataset, allowing performance to be evaluated in terms of detection accuracy and computational efficiency using metrics such as precision, recall, average precision, and inference speed. The results highlight a clear trade-off between efficiency and contextual modeling: CNN-based detectors achieve high performance at a lower computational cost, while transformer-based approaches offer better global context capture at the expense of higher resource demands. These results provide practical criteria for model selection in precision agriculture applications.

### [28] [When Good OCR Is Not Enough: Benchmarking OCR Robustness for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00911)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建覆盖11种挑战类型的文档集；在受控的“OCR优先”的RAG流水线中评测多款SOTA OCR；比较传统OCR指标与下游RAG检索/生成表现，分解错误来源（结构/语义；检索侧/生成侧），并考察在不同OCR优先管线配置下的稳定性。

Result: SOTA OCR在工业场景显著降级；低CER/WER不等价于好RAG性能；结构与语义错误导致显著检索失败与生成错误；类别相关的不匹配显著，且跨典型管线选择稳定存在。

Conclusion: 应超越字符级指标，将结构与语义完整性纳入OCR评估，并以RAG下游任务表现为导向；所提InduOCRBench为公开基准，可推动更鲁棒的工业RAG系统与OCR模型设计。

Abstract: Industrial Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems depend on optical character recognition (OCR) to transform visual documents into text. Existing OCR benchmarks rely on character-level metrics, which inadequately measure downstream RAG effectiveness under real-world conditions. We introduce an OCR benchmark for industrial RAG systems covering 11 challenging document types, including extreme layouts, high-resolution pages, complex or watermarked backgrounds, historical documents with non-standard reading orders, visually decorated text, and documents containing tables and mathematical formulas. Evaluating recent SOTA OCR models under a controlled OCR-first RAG pipeline shows clear performance degradation on realistic industrial documents despite strong conventional benchmark scores. We find that high OCR accuracy does not necessarily translate into strong downstream RAG performance: structural and semantic errors can cause substantial retrieval failures even when WER/CER remains low. Further analysis shows that this mismatch is category-dependent, arises through both retrieval-side and downstream generation-side failures, and remains stable across representative OCR-first pipeline choices. The benchmark is publicly available at https://github.com/Qihoo360/InduOCRBench.

### [29] [Object-Level Explanations for Image Geolocation Models: a GeoGuessr use-case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00912)
*Emilie Durrieu,Christophe Hurter,Philippe Muller,Victor Boutin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出一种面向对象的可解释性管线，用于分析地理定位模型依赖的视觉证据。通过从归因图中提取显著区域并分割成类似“对象”的元素，再用删除/插入测试验证其对预测的贡献，发现归因引导的裁剪比随机裁剪更能保留预测信息，表明归因图可分解为可感知的对象级要素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有地理定位模型的可解释性薄弱：常用的归因方法（如Grad-CAM）往往给出弥散区域，难以对应到清晰的物体或可感知模式，因而无法判断模型是否像人类一样依赖具体对象线索（路面标记、植被、建筑细节）。需要一种能把归因信号转化为对象级证据的分析方法。

Method: 提出对象中心（object-centric）的分析管线：1）从模型的归因图出发，提取显著区域；2）对这些区域进行分割，得到对象样的元素；3）通过删除与插入实验评估其预测相关性——比较“归因引导的裁剪”与“覆盖率相近的随机裁剪”在预测信息保留上的差异。评测在三国分类基准上进行。

Result: 在三国基准实验中，归因引导的裁剪始终比随机裁剪保留更多与模型预测有关的信息，说明这些对象级元素确实承载了关键证据。

Conclusion: 归因图可以被分解为可解释、可感知的对象级成分，支持对地理定位模型进行对象层面的证据分析，为理解模型是否依赖具体可见对象迈出一步。

Abstract: When humans play geolocation games such as GeoGuessr, they rely on concrete visual cues, such as road markings, vegetation, or architectural details, to infer where an image was captured. Whether image geolocation models rely on similar object-level evidence remains difficult to determine, as attribution methods like Grad-CAM typically highlight diffuse regions rather than coherent visual entities, making it difficult to link model predictions to specific objects or perceptible patterns. In this work, we propose an object-centric analysis pipeline to investigate the visual evidence used by geolocation models. Starting from attribution maps, we extract salient regions and segment them into object-like elements. We evaluate their predictive relevance through deletion and insertion tests, comparing attributionguided crops to randomly selected regions with similar coverage. Experiments on a three-country benchmark show that attribution-guided crops consistently retain more information for the model's prediction than random crops. These results suggest that attribution maps can be decomposed into interpretable, perceptible elements, providing a step toward object-level analysis of geolocation models.

### [30] [Leveraging Imperfect Medical Data: A Manifold-Consistent Spatio-Temporal Network for Sensor-based Human Activity Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00913)
*Jiangtao Fan,Anish Jindal,Amir Atapour-Abarghouei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MCSTN，用双重腐化建模与一致性约束，并采用时空双流解耦架构，在PAMAP2、Opportunity、WISDM上，尤其在不完美传感条件下取得SOTA级鲁棒表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实IoMT可穿戴传感存在缺失、故障与噪声，传统深度模型假设输入完备干净，鲁棒性差，需要能在不完美感知下保持识别性能的方法。

Method: 1) 双层腐化建模：物理层腐化（缺测/失效/噪声）+基于扩散的连续腐化，生成多视角受损样本；2) 表征一致性：对多腐化视图施加表示一致性约束，学习稳定、与腐化无关的语义表示；3) 双流时空网络：时间流捕获长期动态，空间流建模传感器间相关性，显式解耦时空学习并融合。

Result: 在PAMAP2、Opportunity、WISDM三基准上取得与SOTA相当或更优的性能，尤其在不完美感知（缺失/噪声）下显著领先。

Conclusion: MCSTN通过真实感的腐化建模与一致性学习，加上时空解耦架构，实现对不完美IoMT信号的鲁棒HAR，适用于现实可穿戴监测场景。

Abstract: Sensor-based Human Activity Recognition (HAR) has attracted increasing attention in medical and healthcare monitoring, particularly with the growth of Internet of Medical Things (IoMT). However, in real-world wearable sensing scenarios, IoMT signals are often corrupted by missing measurements, sensor failures, and environmental noise, which significantly degrade the performance of conventional deep learning models that assume clean and complete inputs. To address this challenge, we propose a Manifold-Consistent Spatio-Temporal Network (MCSTN) for robust HAR under imperfect sensing conditions. The proposed framework introduces a dual-level corruption modeling mechanism that simulates realistic sensor imperfections through both physical-level corruption and diffusion-driven continuous corruption. By enforcing representation consistency across multiple corrupted views, the model learns stable and corruption-invariant semantic representations. Furthermore, we design a dual-stream spatio-temporal architecture that explicitly decouples temporal dynamics modeling and spatial correlation learning. The temporal stream captures long-term activity dynamics, while the spatial stream models inter-sensor relationships, enabling more effective spatio-temporal representation learning. Extensive experiments on three widely used HAR benchmark datasets, PAMAP2, Opportunity, and WISDM, demonstrate that the proposed MCSTN achieves competitive performance compared with existing state-of-the-art methods, particularly under imperfect sensing conditions. These results validate the effectiveness and robustness of the proposed framework for real-world wearable IoMT sensing applications.

### [31] [Rethink MAE with Linear Time-Invariant Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00915)
*Zice Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出SSMProbe，利用状态空间模型作为对视觉表征的顺序敏感探针，证明“token顺序”对冻结视觉模型至关重要，并通过可学习的软排序优于固定扫描策略，在细粒度分类等任务上显著提升表现，同时揭示不同预训练目标导致的token信息异质性与顺序依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有表征探针多用GAP或CLS等置换不变操作，将patch看作无序集合，忽视了可能蕴含在token顺序中的可提取信息。作者希望验证：冻结视觉模型（MAE、BEiT、DINOv2、ViT）中是否存在可被顺序敏感机制利用的结构，并构造一种能诊断与利用该结构的探针方法。

Method: 提出SSMProbe：以离散线性时不变（LTI）状态空间模型作为探针，利用其带记忆衰减的顺序敏感性，使输入token顺序决定最终状态；将token排序视为信息调度问题，比较若干固定扫描启发式与基于Sinkhorn的可微软置换（由下游监督学习）；在标准与细粒度分类上评估不同冻结视觉模型的patch序列。

Result: 存在显著的“顺序差距”：固定扫描在高度局部化patch特征上失败，而学习到的软排序能从局部化序列中提取强竞争力的性能。不同预训练目标塑造了不同的token结构：DINOv2将全局语义集中在优化过的CLS，patch高度专门化；MAE保留分布式表征，patch信息度异质；ViT监督训练呈CLS极端；BEiT介于中间。SSMProbe性能对token在时间位置的布置高度敏感，非仅由空间网格拓扑决定。

Conclusion: token顺序是冻结视觉表征中的关键维度；SSM作为顺序敏感探针能有效诊断并利用预训练模型内部的异质信息分布。通过可学习的软排序，SSMProbe在下游任务中取得显著提升，并为分析不同预训练目标如何塑造token结构提供了新的诊断视角。

Abstract: Standard representation probing for visual models relies on mathematically permutation-invariant operations like Global Average Pooling (GAP) or CLS tokens, treating patch representations as an unstructured bag-of-words. We challenge this paradigm by demonstrating that token order is a critical, exploitable dimension in frozen visual representations (e.g., MAE, BEiT, DINOv2, and ViT as CLS-ablation extreme). We propose SSMProbe, a probing framework driven by a State Space Model (SSM). Operating as discrete Linear Time-Invariant (LTI) dynamical systems, SSMs act as permutation-sensitive probes where sequence order strictly dictates the final state due to inherent memory decay. Formulating token ordering as an information scheduling problem, we compare fixed scan heuristics against a differentiable soft permutation (Sinkhorn-based) learned from downstream supervision. Evaluations on standard and fine-grained classification benchmarks reveal a striking order gap: while fixed scans fail dramatically on highly localized patch features, our learned soft permutation successfully extracts highly competitive performance from otherwise heavily localized patch sequences. We find that pre-training objectives fundamentally shape token structure: DINOv2 concentrates global semantics in optimized CLS tokens leaving patches hyperspecialized, pure MAE preserves distributed representations with heterogeneous patch informativeness, and ViT represents a supervised CLS-dominated extreme. BEiT occupies middle ground. This heterogeneity is order-dependent -- meaning the SSM probe's performance depends critically on which tokens are placed at which temporal positions -- and is not merely a topological property of the spatial grid. SSMProbe's learned routing effectively discovers and exploits this heterogeneity, offering a powerful new diagnostic lens for visual representation analysis.

</details>

Conclusion: 通过将 SAM 的强 2D 边界先验与 Mamba 的 3D 体上下文建模以及跨尺度融合相结合，SAMamba3D 实现了对多相孔隙尺度 X 射线体数据的稳健、可泛化分割，既提升性能又降低适配成本，支撑更可靠、快速的大规模 3D 多相影像分析。

Abstract: Reliable segmentation of multiphase pore-scale X-ray images of rocks is necessary to quantify fluid saturation, connectivity, and interfacial geometry. However, current 3D segmentation methods are typically dataset-specific, requiring retraining or extensive fine-tuning whenever rock type, fluid pattern, scanner, or acquisition conditions change. Foundation models such as the Segment Anything Model (SAM) provide strong 2D boundary priors, but they are not directly applicable to 3D data.
  We present SAMamba3D, a parameter-efficient framework that adapts a largely frozen SAM encoder to generalizable 3D pore-scale segmentation by coupling it with Mamba-based volumetric context modeling and progressive cross-scale feature interaction. For sandstone and carbonate datasets, with different fluids, wettability, and scanning conditions, SAMamba3D matches or outperforms current 3D baselines while reducing the need for case-specific retraining. The resulting segmented images preserve physically meaningful descriptors, including fluid saturation, connectivity, and interface morphology, enabling more reliable and rapid analysis of large 3D multiphase images.

### [33] [Energy-Based Constraint Networks: Learning Structural Coherence Across Modalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00960)
*Chirag Shinde*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种“基于能量的约束网络”（EBCN），在冻结编码器表示上学习结构一致性，通过对比成对数据训练；输出全局能量用于一致性判定与逐位置能量用于定位违规；多分支独立学习不同违规类型并可在推理时可组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨模态/跨编码器地捕捉“结构是否自洽”的通用判别器并能定位不一致处，而无需微调主编码器；现有方法多依赖特定任务/模态或缺少可组合性与可定位能力。

Method: - 用冻结的上游编码器（文本用BERT，视觉用DINOv2）提取特征；
- 通过带双头注意力的状态空间模型生成：1) 全局标量能量（结构一致性度量），2) 逐位置能量（定位违规）；
- 采用对比式训练：干净/受干扰成对样本；
- 多个分支分别在不同“腐化/违规”类型上独立训练，推理时能量可相加组合；
- 研究分支可组合的条件：需要“表示兼容性”。

Result: 文本域：在已训练的腐化类型上93.4%准确率，对9种未见腐化上87.2%，参数量7.4M（冻结BERT）。视觉域（深度伪造检测）：FaceForensics++ Deepfakes AUC=0.959，Celeb-DF零样本AUC=0.870，每分支3.6M参数（冻结DINOv2）。

Conclusion: EBCN以显式能量景观形式学习模态内结构一致性，并能逐位置分解与定位；同一架构仅通过重定义腐化策略即可跨模态迁移；多分支在表示兼容前提下可无干扰组合。

Abstract: We introduce energy-based constraint networks -- a modality-agnostic architecture that learns structural coherence from contrastive pairs. The system processes frozen encoder embeddings through a state-space model with dual-head attention, producing a scalar energy measuring structural consistency alongside per-position energy scores that localize violations. Multiple independently trained branches detect different violation types and compose at inference without interference.
  We demonstrate the framework in two domains. In text, the system achieves 93.4% accuracy on trained corruption types and 87.2% on 9 unseen types, using frozen BERT and 7.4M trainable parameters. In vision, the same architecture achieves competitive deepfake detection: 0.959 AUC on FaceForensics++ Deepfakes and 0.870 on Celeb-DF without any Celeb-DF training data, using frozen DINOv2 and 3.6M parameters per branch.
  The framework supports flexible training: branches learn from designer-specified corruptions, real-world paired data, or both. Composable branches require representation compatibility -- a finding validated through extensive experimentation where five incompatible approaches failed before the compatible one succeeded. The architecture is encoder-agnostic and domain-agnostic: changing the domain requires only new corruption strategies; changing the encoder requires only a new input projection layer. To our knowledge, this is the first architecture to learn within-modality structural coherence as an explicit energy landscape with per-position decomposition, and to demonstrate that the same architecture transfers across modalities via corruption respecification alone.

Conclusion: 开放的数据与管线可显著提升中世纪拉丁手稿的抄录效率与准确率，并通过门户降低研究门槛；传统CNN+LSTM+CTC结合轻量后处理在小数据场景下依然强劲，Transformer OCR易过度猜测而影响可校对性。

Abstract: The record of the beginning of the most widespread legal system in the world is contained in millions of pages of handwritten text. Most of the records of the first centuries of the Anglo-American legal system are hand-written in a highly abbreviated form of medieval Latin which only a few dozen scholars in the world are trained to read. In this interdisciplinary project, we construct a dataset of 4029 lines of text across 193 medieval criminal and civil cases. We then use the dataset to train an open-source end-to-end pipeline for transcribing these manuscripts. We first train standard neural network architectures for line segmentation and handwriting recognition (R-Blla and CNN+LSTM with CTC decoding, respectively) and show that they can already achieve 79% word accuracy, despite the relatively small training set and the challenge of expanding abbreviations. We then demonstrate that simple post-processing significantly boosts accuracy: adding an n-gram language model to the CTC decoder improves word accuracy to 82%, while asking Gemini Pro 3 to correct mistakes boosts accuracy to 88%. Finally, we compare the CNN+LSTM architecture with TrOCR, a transformer-based OCR architecture, demonstrating that TrOCR shows comparable word accuracy but worse character accuracy due to its over-willingness to guess, making it harder for humans to infer the correct reading.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Multimodal Emotion Recognition (MER) is critical for interpreting real-world interactions. In this paper, to systematically investigate these behaviors, we introduce EmoMM, a comprehensive benchmark featuring modality-aligned, conflict, and missing subsets. Through extensive evaluation, we uncover a Video Contribution Collapse (VCC) phenomenon, where MLLM marginalize video evidence due to high token redundancy and modality preferences. To address this, we propose Conflict-aware Head-level Attention Steering (CHASE), a lightweight mechanism that detects modality conflicts and performs inference-time attention steering, effectively mitigating decision bias without retraining the backbone. Experimental results demonstrate that CHASE consistently improves performance across various settings, significantly enhancing the reliability of MLLM in complex affective scenarios.

Extensive experiments show that our approach significantly improves physical plausibility and generalizes well to complex scenes, setting a new benchmark for physically consistent human motion generation.

### [38] [Neighbor2Inverse: Self-Supervised Denoising for Low-Dose Region-of-Interest Phase Contrast CT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01075)
*Johannes B. Thalhammer,Lorenzo D'Amico,Lucy Costello,Sebastian Peterhansl,Daniel Frey,Tina Dorosti,Florian Schaff,Jannis Ahlers,Ronan Smith,Marcus Kitchen,Franz Pfeiffer,Martin Donnelley,Daniela Pfeiffer,Kaye S. Morgan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Neighbor2Inverse自监督去噪框架，通过对每条相位衬度CT投影进行邻域子采样、独立重建并在图像域训练网络，在低剂量PBI-CT中显著抑噪且保留细节，并在临床CT低剂量模拟中具竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PBI-CT具高对比度、医学潜力大，但临床转化受辐射剂量限制；降剂量导致噪声上升。监督去噪需成对低/高剂量数据，实际稀缺；现有自监督方法多不适配PBI-CT这一逆问题。需要一种无需成对数据、契合重建物理与图像域特性的去噪方案。

Method: 基于Neighbor2Neighbor思想：对每条带噪投影进行子采样得到两种保留结构但噪声独立的变体；分别重建得到两幅图像；以其成对训练图像域去噪网络，实现自监督学习。与分析型及多种自监督方法进行基准对比。

Result: 在PBI CT感兴趣区实验中，较基线方法获得更强噪声抑制且保留细微结构，CNR、空间分辨率及复合图像质量指标均提升；在模拟低剂量的临床CT数据上亦表现出有竞争力的性能。

Conclusion: Neighbor2Inverse无需成对数据即可有效去噪低剂量PBI-CT，兼顾细节与分辨率，并可泛化至临床CT，支持低剂量成像的临床可行性。

Abstract: Propagation-based X-ray phase-contrast imaging (PBI) enables high-contrast visualization of lung structures and holds strong medical potential. However, safe translation to the clinic will require a substantial radiation dose reduction, which inevitably increases image noise. Supervised convolutional-neural-network-based denoising can restore image quality but depends on paired low- and high-dose datasets, which are rarely available in practice. Self-supervised methods avoid this limitation, yet most are not well adapted to the inverse problem of PBI computed tomography (CT). We introduce Neighbor2Inverse, a self-supervised denoising framework designed for low-dose PBI-CT that generalizes to clinical CT. Building on the Neighbor2Neighbor principle, each noisy projection is subsampled into two variants that preserve structural information but contain independent noise realizations. These are reconstructed separately, and the resulting pairs are used to train a denoising network directly in the image domain. We benchmark the proposed method against established analytical and self-supervised denoising approaches. In region-of-interest PBI CT experiments, Neighbor2Inverse achieves superior noise suppression while preserving fine structural details, as demonstrated by improved contrast-to-noise ratio, spatial resolution, and composite image quality metrics. Competitive performance is also observed on clinical CT data under simulated low-dose conditions.
  This work has been submitted to the IEEE for possible publication. Copyright may be transferred without notice, after which this version may no longer be accessible.
  Code, data, and interactive figures are available at https://github.com/J-3TO/Neighbor2Inverse.

Abstract: The performance of state-of-the-art object detectors degrades significantly under adverse weather, causing a safety-critical domain shift problem for autonomous vehicles. However, these methods have not been exploited by weather-based domain adaptation approaches due to the noisy nature of such labels generated under harsh weather conditions. ### [40] [Patient-Specific Optimization for Mandibular Reconstruction Planning with Enhanced Bone Union](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01084)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 由术前CT经模板到患者配准，更新肌肉与颞颌关节参数，构建个体化数字孪生；2) 定义以供受骨贴合（apposition）为主、并可加入安全因子正则的目标函数；3) 对6个临床可控的截骨平面与供骨段定位变量，用带EI+采集函数的贝叶斯优化寻优；4) 在通用缺损（体部、颏部、升支-体部）与3+1例患者数据上评估；5) 敏感性分析与纵向随访（与1年骨形成Dice比对）。

Conclusion: OsteoOpt++可在术前由影像驱动给出截骨平面与供骨放置的个性化建议，预计较现行方案改善骨性对合与潜在骨性愈合条件；方法与代码开源，具备临床转化潜力。

Abstract: Mandibular reconstruction with vascularized bone grafts is complicated by donor-host nonunion, and current virtual surgical planning produces a geometric plan rather than a configuration that explicitly promotes bone union. A pre-operative computed tomography (CT) is converted into a personalized digital twin through template-to-patient registration and CT-derived updates of the muscle and temporomandibular-joint parameters. Bayesian optimization with an expected-improvement-plus acquisition rule then searches six clinically controllable cut-plane and donor-positioning variables under an apposition-driven objective and a safety-factor-regularized variant. The workflow was evaluated on three generic defects (body, symphysis, and ramus-body) and a total of 3+1 patient-specific cases, with 3 used for optimization and 1 for validation. In the generic cases, against a common surgical approach, cycle-averaged donor-mandible apposition increased by up to 29 percentage points (329% relative); in the patient-specific cases, against the surgeon-implemented day-5 post-operative configuration, by up to 26 percentage points. A 10% sensitivity analysis over eleven modeling parameters capped the change in the apposition-driven objective at 3% for generic cases and 4% for patient-specific cases, and the longitudinal case showed Dice overlap of 0.70 and 0.76 between predicted apposition and year-1 bone formation. Clinically, this provides surgeons with a pre-operative, image-driven recommendation for cut-plane orientation and donor placement that is predicted to improve union conditions over the configurations currently delivered in the operating room. The optimization and patient-specific modeling code is open source at https://github.com/hamidreza-aftabi/OsteoOpt.
